### Post by michael220 on 2014-10-09
Good morning!  I am an absolute newbie to Linux and Ubuntu and I'm in a bind.

I am running Ubuntu 14.04.1 within the Oracle Virtual Box 4.3.16 on an HP 6000 Pro Desktop with 4 GB RAM.

The issue is with the sizing of the Ubuntu Desktop in VB.  I am unable to resize it to full screen within Virtual Box.

Any ideas on how to resize to full screen?  The screen shot below is the actual size of the Ubuntu window within the Virtual Box.

Any help would be greatly appreciated.

Thanks!

### Post by slickymaster on 2014-10-09
*Moved to the ***Virtualisation**[I] sub-forum
[/I]
Hi michael220, welcome to the forums.

Do you have the VirtualBox guest additions installed? This will give the guest full control of the virtual hardware offered by VirtualBox including the virtual graphics card. With the guest additions installed the guest should resize the resolution of the monitor to whatever the interface window size is or even fullscreen if you want.

---

### Post by ibjsb4 on 2014-10-09
Also be sure to install 'virtualbox-guest-dkms' in the ubuntu guest.

---

### Post by michael220 on 2014-10-09
I have attempted to install the guest additions several times over the last couple of days and I get the attached error....[ATTACH=CONFIG]257066[/ATTACH]

---

### Post by slickymaster on 2014-10-09
It's advisable to install DKMS before installing the Linux Guest Additions. If DKMS is not available or not installed, the guest kernel modules will need to be recreated manually whenever the guest kernel is updated.

On your guest OS, please open a terminal and run the following command:```
sudo apt-get install virtualbox-guest-dkms
```and reboot.

---

Just copy/paste the entire command line from my post into your terminal.
